<td class="mbox-image"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Commons-logo.svg"><img alt="" class="noviewer" data-file-height="1376" data-file-width="1024" height="40" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/30px-Commons-logo.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/45px-Commons-logo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/59px-Commons-logo.svg.png 2x" width="30"/></a></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist">Wikimedia Commons has media related to <i><b><a class="extiw" href="https://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/Category:1932" title="commons:Category:1932">1932</a></b></i>.</td>
</tr>
</table>
<p><b>1932 (<a href="/wiki/Roman_numerals" title="Roman numerals">MCMXXXII</a>)</b> was a <a href="/wiki/Leap_year" title="Leap year">leap year</a> <a href="/wiki/Leap_year_starting_on_Friday" title="Leap year starting on Friday">starting on Friday</a> (<a href="/wiki/Dominical_letter" title="Dominical letter">dominical letter</a> CB) of the <a href="/wiki/Gregorian_calendar" title="Gregorian calendar">Gregorian calendar</a>, the 1932nd year of the <a href="/wiki/Common_Era" title="Common Era">Common Era</a> (CE) and <i><a href="/wiki/Anno_Domini" title="Anno Domini">Anno Domini</a></i> (AD) designations, the 932nd year of the <a href="/wiki/2nd_millennium" title="2nd millennium">2nd millennium</a>, the 32nd year of the <a href="/wiki/20th_century" title="20th century">20th century</a>, and the 3rd year of the <a href="/wiki/1930s" title="1930s">1930s</a> decade.</p>
<div class="toclimit-2">

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Events">Events</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Events">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="January">January</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: January">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/January_1932" title="January 1932">January 1932</a></div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_1" title="January 1">January 1</a> – The United States Post Office Department issues <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/1932_Washington_Bicentennial" title="1932 Washington Bicentennial">a set of 12 stamps</a> commemorating the 200th anniversary of <a href="/wiki/George_Washington" title="George Washington">George Washington</a>'s birth.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_3" title="January 3">January 3</a> – The British arrest and intern <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mohandas_Gandhi" title="Mohandas Gandhi">Mohandas Gandhi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Vallabhbhai_Patel" title="Vallabhbhai Patel">Vallabhbhai Patel</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_7" title="January 7">January 7</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Stimson_Doctrine" title="Stimson Doctrine">Stimson Doctrine</a> is proclaimed, in response to the Japanese invasion of <a href="/wiki/Manchuria" title="Manchuria">Manchuria</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_8" title="January 8">January 8</a> – In Great Britain the <a href="/wiki/Cosmo_Gordon_Lang" title="Cosmo Gordon Lang">Archbishop of Canterbury</a> forbids Anglican church remarriage of divorced persons.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_9" title="January 9">January 9</a> – <a href="/wiki/Sakuradamon_Incident_(1932)" title="Sakuradamon Incident (1932)">Sakuradamon Incident</a>, Korean nationalist <a href="/wiki/Lee_Bong-chang" title="Lee Bong-chang">Lee Bong-chang</a> fails in his effort to assassinate <a href="/wiki/Hirohito" title="Hirohito">Hirohito</a> Emperor of Japan. The <a href="/wiki/Kuomintang" title="Kuomintang">Kuomintang</a>'s official newspaper runs an editorial expressing regret that the attempt failed, which is used by the Japanese as a pretext to attack Shanghai later in the month.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_12" title="January 12">January 12</a> – <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hattie_W._Caraway" title="Hattie W. Caraway">Hattie W. Caraway</a> becomes the first woman elected to the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Senate" title="United States Senate">United States Senate</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_14" title="January 14">January 14</a> – <a href="/wiki/Maurice_Ravel" title="Maurice Ravel">Maurice Ravel</a>'s <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Concerto_in_G_(Ravel)" title="Concerto in G (Ravel)">Concerto in G</a> debuts with piano soloist <a href="/wiki/Marguerite_Long" title="Marguerite Long">Marguerite Long</a> and Ravel conducting the Lamoureux Orchestra.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_15" title="January 15">January 15</a> – About 6 million are unemployed in Germany.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_22" title="January 22">January 22</a> – The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/1932_Salvadoran_peasant_uprising" title="1932 Salvadoran peasant uprising">1932 Salvadoran peasant uprising</a> begins, it is suppressed by the government of <a href="/wiki/Maximiliano_Hern%C3%A1ndez_Mart%C3%ADnez" title="Maximiliano Hernández Martínez">Maximiliano Hernández Martínez</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_24" title="January 24">January 24</a> – Marshal <a href="/wiki/Pietro_Badoglio" title="Pietro Badoglio">Pietro Badoglio</a> declares the end of <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libyan</a> resistance.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_26" title="January 26">January 26</a> – The British submarine <a href="/wiki/HMS_M2" title="HMS M2"><i>M2</i></a> sinks with all 60 hands.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_28" title="January 28">January 28</a> – Conflict between Japan and China in the <a href="/wiki/January_28_Incident" title="January 28 Incident">Battle of Shanghai</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_29" title="January 29">January 29</a> – The minority government of <a href="/wiki/Karl_Buresch" title="Karl Buresch">Karl Buresch</a> in Austria ends the governmental crisis.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_31" title="January 31">January 31</a> – Japanese warships arrive in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nanking" title="Nanking">Nanking</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="February">February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:233px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:1932_Winter_Olympics_logo.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="370" data-file-width="231" height="370" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/4/4f/1932_Winter_Olympics_logo.png" width="231"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:1932_Winter_Olympics_logo.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/1932_Winter_Olympics" title="1932 Winter Olympics">1932 Winter Olympics</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/February_1932" title="February 1932">February 1932</a></div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_1" title="February 1">February 1</a> – <i><a href="/wiki/Brave_New_World" title="Brave New World">Brave New World</a></i>, a novel by <a href="/wiki/Aldous_Huxley" title="Aldous Huxley">Aldous Huxley</a>, is first published.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_2" title="February 2">February 2</a>
<ul>
<li>A general <a href="/wiki/World_Disarmament_Conference" title="World Disarmament Conference">World Disarmament Conference</a> begins in <a href="/wiki/Geneva" title="Geneva">Geneva</a>. The principal issue at the conference is the demand made by Germany for <i>gleichberechtigung</i> ("equality of status" i.e. abolishing Part V of the Treaty of Versailles, which had disarmed Germany) and the French demand for <i>sécurité</i> ("security" i.e. maintaining Part V).</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/League_of_Nations" title="League of Nations">League of Nations</a> again recommends negotiations between the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_China_(1912%E2%80%9349)" title="Republic of China (1912–49)">Republic of China</a> and Japan.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Reconstruction_Finance_Corporation" title="Reconstruction Finance Corporation">Reconstruction Finance Corporation</a> begins operations in Washington, D.C.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_4" title="February 4">February 4</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/1932_Winter_Olympics" title="1932 Winter Olympics">1932 Winter Olympics</a> open in <a href="/wiki/Lake_Placid,_New_York" title="Lake Placid, New York">Lake Placid, New York</a>.</li>
<li>Japan occupies <a href="/wiki/Harbin" title="Harbin">Harbin</a>, China.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_9" title="February 9">February 9</a> – <a href="/wiki/Junnosuke_Inoue" title="Junnosuke Inoue">Junnosuke Inoue</a>, prominent Japanese businessman, banker and former governor of the Bank of Japan is assassinated by right-wing extremist group the League of Blood in the <a href="/wiki/League_of_Blood_Incident" title="League of Blood Incident">League of Blood Incident</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_11" title="February 11">February 11</a> – <a href="/wiki/Pope_Pius_XI" title="Pope Pius XI">Pope Pius XI</a> meets <a href="/wiki/Benito_Mussolini" title="Benito Mussolini">Benito Mussolini</a> in <a href="/wiki/Vatican_City" title="Vatican City">Vatican City</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_15" title="February 15">February 15</a> – <i>Clara, Lu &amp; Em</i>, generally regarded as the first daytime network <a href="/wiki/Soap_opera" title="Soap opera">soap opera</a>, debuts in its morning time slot over the <a href="/wiki/Blue_Network" title="Blue Network">Blue Network</a> of <a href="/wiki/NBC" title="NBC">NBC</a> Radio, having originally been a late evening program.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_18" title="February 18">February 18</a> – Japan declares <a href="/wiki/Manchukuo" title="Manchukuo">Manchukuo</a> (Japanese name for <a href="/wiki/Manchuria" title="Manchuria">Manchuria</a>) formally independent from China.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_22" title="February 22">February 22</a> – The first <a href="/wiki/Purple_Heart" title="Purple Heart">Purple Heart</a> is awarded.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_24" title="February 24">February 24</a> – <a href="/wiki/Women%27s_suffrage" title="Women's suffrage">Women's suffrage</a> is granted in Brazil.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_25" title="February 25">February 25</a> – <a href="/wiki/Adolf_Hitler" title="Adolf Hitler">Adolf Hitler</a> obtains German citizenship by <a href="/wiki/Naturalization" title="Naturalization">naturalization</a>, opening the opportunity for him to run in the 1932 election for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Reichspr%C3%A4sident" title="Reichspräsident">Reichspräsident</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_27" title="February 27">February 27</a> – The <a href="/wiki/M%C3%A4nts%C3%A4l%C3%A4_rebellion" title="Mäntsälä rebellion">Mäntsälä rebellion</a> occurs in Finland.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="March">March</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: March">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/March_1932" title="March 1932">March 1932</a></div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_1" title="March 1">March 1</a>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Charles_Lindbergh,_Jr." title="Charles Lindbergh, Jr.">Charles Lindbergh, Jr.</a>, the infant son of <a href="/wiki/Anne_Morrow_Lindbergh" title="Anne Morrow Lindbergh">Anne Morrow Lindbergh</a> and <a href="/wiki/Charles_Lindbergh" title="Charles Lindbergh">Charles Lindbergh</a>, is kidnapped from the family home near <a href="/wiki/Hopewell,_New_Jersey" title="Hopewell, New Jersey">Hopewell, New Jersey</a>.</li>
<li>Japan proclaims <a href="/wiki/Manchuria" title="Manchuria">Manchuria</a> an independent state and installs <a href="/wiki/Puyi" title="Puyi">Puyi</a> as <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Puppet_emperor" title="Puppet emperor">puppet emperor</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_2" title="March 2">March 2</a> – The <a href="/wiki/M%C3%A4nts%C3%A4l%C3%A4_rebellion" title="Mäntsälä rebellion">Mäntsälä rebellion</a> ends in failure; Finnish democracy prevails. The <a href="/wiki/Lapua_Movement" title="Lapua Movement">Lapua Movement</a> is condemned by conservative Finnish President <a href="/wiki/Pehr_Evind_Svinhufvud" title="Pehr Evind Svinhufvud">Pehr Evind Svinhufvud</a> in a radio speech.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_5" title="March 5">March 5</a> – <a href="/wiki/Dan_Takuma" title="Dan Takuma">Dan Takuma</a>, prominent Japanese businessman and director of the <a href="/wiki/Mitsui" title="Mitsui">Mitsui</a> <i><a href="/wiki/Zaibatsu" title="Zaibatsu">Zaibatsu</a></i> conglomerate is assassinated by the radical right-wing League of Blood group.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_7" title="March 7">March 7</a> – Four people are killed when police fire upon 3,000 unemployed autoworkers marching outside the <a href="/wiki/Ford_Motor_Company" title="Ford Motor Company">Ford</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/River_Rouge_Plant" title="River Rouge Plant">River Rouge Plant</a> in <a href="/wiki/Dearborn,_Michigan" title="Dearborn, Michigan">Dearborn, Michigan</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_9" title="March 9">March 9</a> – <a href="/wiki/%C3%89amon_de_Valera" title="Éamon de Valera">Éamon de Valera</a> is elected <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_Executive_Council_of_the_Irish_Free_State" title="President of the Executive Council of the Irish Free State">President of the Executive Council</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Irish_Free_State" title="Irish Free State">Irish Free State</a>. It is the first change of government in the Irish Free State since its foundation 10 years previously.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_14" title="March 14">March 14</a> – <a href="/wiki/George_Eastman" title="George Eastman">George Eastman</a>, founder of <a href="/wiki/Kodak" title="Kodak">Kodak</a>, commits suicide.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_18" title="March 18">March 18</a> – Peace negotiations between China and Japan begin.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_19" title="March 19">March 19</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Sydney_Harbour_Bridge" title="Sydney Harbour Bridge">Sydney Harbour Bridge</a> opens.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_20" title="March 20">March 20</a> – The <i><a href="/wiki/LZ_127_Graf_Zeppelin" title="LZ 127 Graf Zeppelin">Graf Zeppelin</a></i> begins a regular route to South America.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_21" title="March 21">March 21</a>– A series of deadly tornadoes in the south kills more than 220 people in <a href="/wiki/Alabama" title="Alabama">Alabama</a>, 34 in <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(U.S._state)" title="Georgia (U.S. state)">Georgia</a> and 17 in <a href="/wiki/Tennessee" title="Tennessee">Tennessee</a> during a two-day period.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_25" title="March 25">March 25</a> – <i><a href="/wiki/Tarzan_the_Ape_Man_(1932_film)" title="Tarzan the Ape Man (1932 film)">Tarzan the Ape Man</a></i> opens, with Olympic gold medal swimmer <a href="/wiki/Johnny_Weissmuller" title="Johnny Weissmuller">Johnny Weissmuller</a> in the title role. (Weismuller will star in a total of twelve <i><a href="/wiki/Tarzan" title="Tarzan">Tarzan</a></i> films.)</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="April">April</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: April">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/April_1932" title="April 1932">April 1932</a></div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_5" title="April 5">April 5</a>
<ul>
<li>10,000 disgruntled Newfoundlanders march on their legislature to show discontent with their current political situation; this is a flash point in the demise of the <a href="/wiki/Dominion_of_Newfoundland" title="Dominion of Newfoundland">Dominion of Newfoundland</a>.</li>
<li><i>Kreuger &amp; Toll</i>, the company of the "Match King" <a href="/wiki/Ivar_Kreuger" title="Ivar Kreuger">Ivar Kreuger</a>, collapses.</li>
<li>The first <a href="/wiki/Alko" title="Alko">Alko</a> stores are opened in Finland at 10 in the morning (local time) following the end of Prohibition in that country, resulting in a new <a href="/wiki/Mnemonic" title="Mnemonic">mnemonic</a> "543210".</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_6" title="April 6">April 6</a>
<ul>
<li>U.S. president <a href="/wiki/Herbert_Hoover" title="Herbert Hoover">Herbert Hoover</a> supports armament limitations at the World Disarmament Conference.</li>
<li>The trial against fraudulent art dealer <a href="/wiki/Otto_Wacker" title="Otto Wacker">Otto Wacker</a> begins in Berlin.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_11" title="April 11">April 11</a> – <a href="/wiki/Paul_von_Hindenburg" title="Paul von Hindenburg">Paul von Hindenburg</a> is re-elected president of Germany.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_13" title="April 13">April 13</a> – German Chancellor <a href="/wiki/Heinrich_Br%C3%BCning" title="Heinrich Brüning">Heinrich Brüning</a> bans the <a href="/wiki/Sturmabteilung" title="Sturmabteilung">SA</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Schutzstaffel" title="Schutzstaffel">SS</a> as threats to public order, arguing that they are chiefly responsible for the wave of political violence afflicting Germany.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Feuchtwanger_1-0"><a href="#cite_note-Feuchtwanger-1">[1]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_14" title="April 14">April 14</a> – <a href="/wiki/John_Cockcroft" title="John Cockcroft">John Cockcroft</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ernest_Walton" title="Ernest Walton">Ernest Walton</a> focus a proton beam on lithium and split its nucleus.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_17" title="April 17">April 17</a> – <a href="/wiki/Haile_Selassie" title="Haile Selassie">Haile Selassie</a> announces an anti-<a href="/wiki/Slavery" title="Slavery">slavery</a> law in <a href="/wiki/Ethiopia" title="Ethiopia">Abyssinia</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_19" title="April 19">April 19</a> – German art dealer <a href="/wiki/Otto_Wacker" title="Otto Wacker">Otto Wacker</a> is sentenced to 19 months in prison for selling <a href="/wiki/Art_forgery" title="Art forgery">fraudulent</a> paintings he attributed to <a href="/wiki/Vincent_van_Gogh" title="Vincent van Gogh">Vincent van Gogh</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_25" title="April 25">April 25</a> – Two of the companions of Islamic prophet <a href="/wiki/Muhammad" title="Muhammad">Muhammad</a> are moved from their graves upon informing of water in the graves in the dream of <a href="/wiki/Faisal_I_of_Iraq" title="Faisal I of Iraq">King Faisal</a> of <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a> in Salmaan Paak, Iraq. Their names are <a href="/wiki/Hudhayfah_ibn_al-Yaman" title="Hudhayfah ibn al-Yaman">Hudhayfah ibn al-Yaman</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jabir_ibn_Abd_Allah" title="Jabir ibn Abd Allah">Jabir ibn Abd Allah</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_29" title="April 29">April 29</a> – Korean pro-independence paramilitary <a href="/wiki/Yun_Bong-gil" title="Yun Bong-gil">Yun Bong-gil</a> detonates a bomb at a gathering of Japanese government and mililtary officials in <a href="/wiki/Shanghai" title="Shanghai">Shanghai</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Lu_Xun_Park_(Shanghai)" title="Lu Xun Park (Shanghai)">Hongkou Park</a>, killing General <a href="/wiki/Yoshinori_Shirakawa" title="Yoshinori Shirakawa">Yoshinori Shirakawa</a> and injuring <a href="/wiki/Mamoru_Shigemitsu" title="Mamoru Shigemitsu">Mamoru Shigemitsu</a> and Vice Admiral <a href="/wiki/Kichisabur%C5%8D_Nomura" title="Kichisaburō Nomura">Kichisaburō Nomura</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="May">May</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: May">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/May_1932" title="May 1932">May 1932</a></div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_2" title="May 2">May 2</a> – Comedian <a href="/wiki/Jack_Benny" title="Jack Benny">Jack Benny</a>'s radio show airs for the first time.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_6" title="May 6">May 6</a> – <a href="/wiki/Paul_Gorguloff" title="Paul Gorguloff">Paul Gorguloff</a> shoots French president <a href="/wiki/Paul_Doumer" title="Paul Doumer">Paul Doumer</a> in Paris; Doumer dies the next day.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_6" title="May 6">May 6</a> – The politically powerful General <a href="/wiki/Kurt_von_Schleicher" title="Kurt von Schleicher">Kurt von Schleicher</a> meets secretly with <a href="/wiki/Adolf_Hitler" title="Adolf Hitler">Adolf Hitler</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto_2-0"><a href="#cite_note-auto-2">[2]</a></sup> Schleicher tells Hitler that he is scheming to bring down the Brüning government and asks for Nazi support of the new "presidential government" Schleicher is planning to form.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto_2-1"><a href="#cite_note-auto-2">[2]</a></sup> Schleicher and Hitler negotiated a "gentlemen's agreement" where in exchange for lifting the ban on the SA and SS and having the <i>Reichstag</i> dissolved for early elections that summer, the Nazis will support Schleicher's new chancellor.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_10" title="May 10">May 10</a>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Albert_Lebrun" title="Albert Lebrun">Albert Lebrun</a> becomes the new <a href="/wiki/President_of_France" title="President of France">president of France</a>.</li>
<li>Violent scenes in the <i>Reichstag</i> as <a href="/wiki/Hermann_G%C3%B6ring" title="Hermann Göring">Hermann Göring</a> and other Nazi MRDs attack the Defense Minister General <a href="/wiki/Wilhelm_Groener" title="Wilhelm Groener">Wilhelm Groener</a> for his lack of belief in a supposed Social Democratic <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Putsch" title="Putsch">putsch</a></i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto_2-2"><a href="#cite_note-auto-2">[2]</a></sup> After the debate, General Schleicher tells Groener that he has lost the confidence of the Army and must resign at once.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto_2-3"><a href="#cite_note-auto-2">[2]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_12" title="May 12">May 12</a>
<ul>
<li>Ten weeks after his abduction, the infant son of <a href="/wiki/Charles_Lindbergh" title="Charles Lindbergh">Charles Lindbergh</a> is found dead just a few miles from the Lindbergh home.</li>
<li>General Wilhelm Groener resigns as Defense Minister.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto_2-4"><a href="#cite_note-auto-2">[2]</a></sup> Schleicher takes control of the Defense Ministry.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_13" title="May 13">May 13</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Premier_of_New_South_Wales" title="Premier of New South Wales">Premier of New South Wales</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jack_Lang_(Australian_politician)" title="Jack Lang (Australian politician)">Jack Lang</a>, is dismissed by the State Governor, Sir <a href="/wiki/Philip_Game" title="Philip Game">Philip Game</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_15" title="May 15">May 15</a> – Japanese troops leave Shanghai. Back in Japan, the <a href="/wiki/May_15_Incident" title="May 15 Incident">May 15 Incident</a> as an attempted military coup is known occurs. The Japanese prime minister <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tsuyoshi_Inukai" title="Tsuyoshi Inukai">Tsuyoshi Inukai</a> is assassinated by naval officers.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_16" title="May 16">May 16</a> – Massive riots between Hindus and Muslims in <a href="/wiki/Mumbai" title="Mumbai">Bombay</a> leave thousands dead and injured.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_20" title="May 20">May 20</a>–<a href="/wiki/May_21" title="May 21">May 21</a> – <a href="/wiki/Amelia_Earhart" title="Amelia Earhart">Amelia Earhart</a> flies from the United States to <a href="/wiki/County_Londonderry" title="County Londonderry">County Londonderry</a>, <a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland" title="Northern Ireland">Northern Ireland</a> in 14 hours 54 minutes.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_20" title="May 20">May 20</a> – <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Federaci%C3%B3n_Obrera_de_la_Industria_de_la_Carne" title="Federación Obrera de la Industria de la Carne">Federación Obrera de la Industria de la Carne</a></i> initiates a major <a href="/wiki/Strike_action" title="Strike action">strike</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentinian</a> meat-packing industry.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_26" title="May 26">May 26</a> – Judgement in <a href="/wiki/Donoghue_v_Stevenson" title="Donoghue v Stevenson">Donoghue v Stevenson</a> handed down in the <a href="/wiki/House_of_Lords" title="House of Lords">House of Lords</a>, creating the neighbour principle in English law.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_29" title="May 29">May 29</a> – The first of approximately 15,000 <a href="/wiki/World_War_I" title="World War I">World War I</a> veterans arrive in <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">Washington, D.C.</a> demanding the immediate payment of their military bonus, becoming known as the <a href="/wiki/Bonus_Army" title="Bonus Army">Bonus Army</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_30" title="May 30">May 30</a> – German chancellor <a href="/wiki/Heinrich_Br%C3%BCning" title="Heinrich Brüning">Heinrich Brüning</a> is dismissed by President von Hindenburg. President Hindenburg asks <a href="/wiki/Franz_von_Papen" title="Franz von Papen">Franz von Papen</a> to form a new government, known as the "Government of the President's Friends", which is openly dedicated to the destruction of democracy and the <a href="/wiki/Weimar_Republic" title="Weimar Republic">Weimar Republic</a>. The downfall of Brüning is largely the work of Schleicher, who been scheming against him since the beginning of May.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Feuchtwanger_1-1"><a href="#cite_note-Feuchtwanger-1">[1]</a></sup> Schleicher takes the position of Defense Minister in his friend Papen's government.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="June">June</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: June">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/June_1932" title="June 1932">June 1932</a></div>
<ul>
<li>June – The <a href="/wiki/Chaco_War" title="Chaco War">Chaco War</a> begins between <a href="/wiki/Bolivia" title="Bolivia">Bolivia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Paraguay" title="Paraguay">Paraguay</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_4" title="June 4">June 4</a>
<ul>
<li>A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Military_coup" title="Military coup">military coup</a> occurs in <a href="/wiki/Chile" title="Chile">Chile</a>.</li>
<li>The Papen government dissolves the <i>Reichstag</i> for elections on 31 July 1932 in the full expectation that the Nazis will win the largest number of seats.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_6" title="June 6">June 6</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Revenue_Act_of_1932" title="Revenue Act of 1932">Revenue Act of 1932</a> is enacted, creating the first <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Gas_tax" title="Gas tax">gas tax</a> in the United States at 1 cent per US gallon (0.26 ¢/L) sold.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_14" title="June 14">June 14</a> – The Papen government lifts the ban against the SS and <a href="/wiki/Sturmabteilung" title="Sturmabteilung">SA</a> in Germany.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_16" title="June 16">June 16</a>– <a href="/wiki/Lausanne_Conference_of_1932" title="Lausanne Conference of 1932">Lausanne conference</a> opens to discuss <a href="/wiki/World_War_I_reparations" title="World War I reparations">reparations</a>, which Germany had not paying since the <a href="/wiki/Hoover_Moratorium" title="Hoover Moratorium">Hoover Moratorium</a> of June 1931.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_20" title="June 20">June 20</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Benelux" title="Benelux">Benelux</a> customs union is negotiated.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_24" title="June 24">June 24</a> – After a relatively bloodless military rebellion, <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Siam</a> becomes a <a href="/wiki/Constitutional_monarchy" title="Constitutional monarchy">constitutional monarchy</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_25" title="June 25">June 25</a> – <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a> played its first <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Test_Cricket" title="Test Cricket">Test Cricket</a> Match with <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a> at <a href="/wiki/Lord%27s" title="Lord's">Lord's</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_29" title="June 29">June 29</a> – The comedy serial <i><a href="/wiki/Vic_and_Sade" title="Vic and Sade">Vic and Sade</a></i> debuts on <a href="/wiki/NBC" title="NBC">NBC</a> Radio.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="July">July</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: July">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:242px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:1932_Summer_Olympics_logo.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="370" data-file-width="355" height="250" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/5/5d/1932_Summer_Olympics_logo.png/240px-1932_Summer_Olympics_logo.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/5/5d/1932_Summer_Olympics_logo.png 1.5x" width="240"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:1932_Summer_Olympics_logo.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/1932_Summer_Olympics" title="1932 Summer Olympics">1932 Summer Olympics</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/July_1932" title="July 1932">July 1932</a></div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_5" title="July 5">July 5</a> – <a href="/wiki/Ant%C3%B3nio_de_Oliveira_Salazar" title="António de Oliveira Salazar">António de Oliveira Salazar</a> becomes the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fascist" title="Fascist">fascist</a> prime minister of Portugal (for the next 36 years).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_7" title="July 7">July 7</a> – The French submarine <i><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Prom%C3%A9th%C3%A9e_(Q153)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Prométhée (Q153) (page does not exist)">Prométhée</a></i> sinks off <a href="/wiki/Cherbourg-Octeville" title="Cherbourg-Octeville">Cherbourg</a>; 66 are killed.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_8" title="July 8">July 8</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Dow_Jones_Industrial_Average" title="Dow Jones Industrial Average">Dow Jones Industrial Average</a> reaches its lowest level of the <a href="/wiki/Great_Depression" title="Great Depression">Great Depression</a>, bottoming out at 41.22.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_9" title="July 9">July 9</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Constitutionalist_Revolution" title="Constitutionalist Revolution">Constitutionalist Revolution</a> starts in Brazil, with the uprising of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/State_of_S%C3%A3o_Paulo" title="State of São Paulo">state of São Paulo</a>.</li>
<li>Lausanne conference ends, agrees to cancel <a href="/wiki/World_War_I_reparations" title="World War I reparations">reparations</a> against Germany.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_12" title="July 12">July 12</a>
<ul>
<li>Norway annexes northern <a href="/wiki/Greenland" title="Greenland">Greenland</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hedley_Verity" title="Hedley Verity">Hedley Verity</a> establishes a new <a href="/wiki/First-class_cricket" title="First-class cricket">first-class cricket</a> record by taking all ten wickets for only ten runs against Nottinghamshire on a pitch affected by a storm.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_17" title="July 17">July 17</a> – <a href="/wiki/Altona_Bloody_Sunday" title="Altona Bloody Sunday">Altona Bloody Sunday</a>: In Altona, Germany, armed <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Communist" title="Communist">communists</a> attack a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/National_Socialist_German_Workers_Party" title="National Socialist German Workers Party">National Socialist</a> demonstration; 18 are killed and many other political street fights follow.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_20" title="July 20">July 20</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Preu%C3%9Fenschlag" title="Preußenschlag">Preußenschlag</a> in Germany. The Papen government sends out the <i>Reichswehr</i> under General <a href="/wiki/Gerd_von_Rundstedt" title="Gerd von Rundstedt">Gerd von Rundstedt</a> to depose the elected SPD government in Prussia under <a href="/wiki/Otto_Braun" title="Otto Braun">Otto Braun</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup> The coup gives Papen control of Prussia, the most powerful <i>Land</i> in Germany, and is a major blow to German democracy.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_21" title="July 21">July 21</a> – <a href="/wiki/British_Empire_Economic_Conference" title="British Empire Economic Conference">British Empire Economic Conference</a> opens in Ottawa, Canada.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_28" title="July 28">July 28</a> – U.S. President <a href="/wiki/Herbert_Hoover" title="Herbert Hoover">Herbert Hoover</a> orders the U.S. Army to forcibly evict the <a href="/wiki/Bonus_Army" title="Bonus Army">Bonus Army</a> of World War I veterans gathered in Washington, D.C. Troops disperse the last of the Bonus Army the next day.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_30" title="July 30">July 30</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/1932_Summer_Olympics" title="1932 Summer Olympics">1932 Summer Olympics</a> open in <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles" title="Los Angeles">Los Angeles</a>.</li>
<li>Walt Disney's <i><a href="/wiki/Flowers_and_Trees" title="Flowers and Trees">Flowers and Trees</a></i>, the first animated cartoon to be presented in full <a href="/wiki/Technicolor" title="Technicolor">Technicolor</a>, premieres in Los Angeles. It releases in theaters, along with <a href="/wiki/Strange_Interlude_(film)" title="Strange Interlude (film)">the film version</a> of <a href="/wiki/Eugene_O%27Neill" title="Eugene O'Neill">Eugene O'Neill</a>'s <i><a href="/wiki/Strange_Interlude" title="Strange Interlude">Strange Interlude</a></i> (starring <a href="/wiki/Norma_Shearer" title="Norma Shearer">Norma Shearer</a> and <a href="/wiki/Clark_Gable" title="Clark Gable">Clark Gable</a>); <i>Flowers and Trees</i> goes on to win the first Academy Award for Best Animated Short.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_31" title="July 31">July 31</a> – <a href="/wiki/German_federal_election,_July_1932" title="German federal election, July 1932"><i>Reichstag</i> election</a> sees the Nazis win 37% of the vote, becoming the largest party in the <i>Reichstag</i>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="August">August</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: August">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/August_1932" title="August 1932">August 1932</a></div>
<ul>
<li>August – A farmers' revolt begins in the <a href="/wiki/Midwestern_United_States" title="Midwestern United States">Midwestern United States</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_1" title="August 1">August 1</a>
<ul>
<li>The second <a href="/wiki/International_Polar_Year" title="International Polar Year">International Polar Year</a>, an international scientific collaboration, begins.</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Forrest_Edward_Mars,_Sr." title="Forrest Edward Mars, Sr.">Forrest Mars</a> produces the first <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mars_bar" title="Mars bar">Mars bar</a> in his <a href="/wiki/Slough" title="Slough">Slough</a> factory in England.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_2" title="August 2">August 2</a> – The first <a href="/wiki/Positron" title="Positron">positron</a> is discovered by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Carl_D._Anderson" title="Carl D. Anderson">Carl D. Anderson</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_5" title="August 5">August 5</a> – Hitler meets with Schleicher and reneges on the "gentlemen's agreement", demanding that he be appointed Chancellor.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup> Schleicher agrees to support Hitler as Chancellor provided that he can remain minister of defense.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup> Schleicher sets up a meeting between Hindenburg and Hitler on for the 13 August to discuss Hitler's possible appointment as chancellor.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_6" title="August 6">August 6</a>
<ul>
<li>The first <a href="/wiki/Venice_Film_Festival" title="Venice Film Festival">Venice Film Festival</a> is held.</li>
<li>In Germany the first worldwide <a href="/wiki/Autobahn" title="Autobahn">Autobahn</a> opened by <a href="/wiki/Konrad_Adenauer" title="Konrad Adenauer">Konrad Adenauer</a>: <a href="/wiki/Bundesautobahn_555" title="Bundesautobahn 555">Bundesautobahn 555</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Carl_Gustaf_Ekman" title="Carl Gustaf Ekman">Carl Gustaf Ekman</a> resigns as <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Sweden" title="Prime Minister of Sweden">Prime Minister</a> of <a href="/wiki/Sweden" title="Sweden">Sweden</a>, and is replaced by his Minister of Finance <a href="/wiki/Felix_Hamrin" title="Felix Hamrin">Felix Hamrin</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_7" title="August 7">August 7</a> – Raymond Edward Welch becomes the first one legged man to scale the 6,288 ft. <a href="/wiki/Mount_Washington_(New_Hampshire)" title="Mount Washington (New Hampshire)">Mount Washington, New Hampshire</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_9" title="August 9">August 9</a>
<ul>
<li>The Papen government in Germany, which likes to take a tough "law and order" stance, passes via Article 48 a law proscribing the death penalty for a variety of offenses and with the court system simplified so that the courts can hand down as many death sentences as possible.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto1_9-0"><a href="#cite_note-auto1-9">[9]</a></sup></li>
<li>The Potempa Murder case: In the German town of <a href="/wiki/Pot%C4%99pa" title="Potępa">Potempa</a>, five Nazi "<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Brownshirts" title="Brownshirts">Brownshirts</a>" break into the house of Konrad Pietrzuch, a Communist miner, and proceed to castrate and beat him to death in front of his mother.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup> The case attracts much media attention in Germany. The murderers were released from jail after <a href="/wiki/Adolf_Hitler" title="Adolf Hitler">Adolf Hitler</a> became <a href="/wiki/Chancellor_of_Germany" title="Chancellor of Germany">Chancellor of Germany</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_10" title="August 10">August 10</a> – A 5.1 kg <a href="/wiki/Chondrite" title="Chondrite">chondrite</a>-type <a href="/wiki/Meteorite" title="Meteorite">meteorite</a> breaks fragments and strikes earth near the town of <a href="/wiki/Archie,_Missouri" title="Archie, Missouri">Archie, Missouri</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_11" title="August 11">August 11</a> – To celebrate Constitution Day in Germany, Chancellor <a href="/wiki/Franz_von_Papen" title="Franz von Papen">Franz von Papen</a> and his interior minister Baron <a href="/wiki/Wilhelm_von_Gayl" title="Wilhelm von Gayl">Wilhelm von Gayl</a> present proposed amendments to the Weimar constitution for a "New State" to deal with the problems besetting Germany.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto2_12-0"><a href="#cite_note-auto2-12">[12]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_13" title="August 13">August 13</a> – Hitler meets President von Hindenburg and asks to be appointed as Chancellor.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup> Hindenburg refuses under the grounds that Hitler is not qualified to be Chancellor and asks him instead to serve as Vice-Chancellor in Papen's government.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto2_12-1"><a href="#cite_note-auto2-12">[12]</a></sup> Hitler announces his "all or nothing" strategy in which he will oppose any government not headed by himself and will accept no office other than Chancellor.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_18" title="August 18">August 18</a> – <a href="/wiki/Auguste_Piccard" title="Auguste Piccard">Auguste Piccard</a> reaches an altitude of 16,197 m (53,140 ft) with a <a href="/wiki/Hot_air_balloon" title="Hot air balloon">hot air balloon</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_18" title="August 18">August 18</a>–<a href="/wiki/August_19" title="August 19">19</a> – Scottish aviator <a href="/wiki/Jim_Mollison" title="Jim Mollison">Jim Mollison</a> becomes the first pilot to make an East-to-West solo <a href="/wiki/Transatlantic_flight" title="Transatlantic flight">transatlantic flight</a>, from <a href="/wiki/Portmarnock" title="Portmarnock">Portmarnock</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dublin" title="Dublin">Dublin</a>, Ireland to <a href="/wiki/RCAF_Station_Pennfield_Ridge" title="RCAF Station Pennfield Ridge">Pennfield</a>, <a href="/wiki/New_Brunswick" title="New Brunswick">New Brunswick</a>, Canada, in his <a href="/wiki/De_Havilland_Puss_Moth" title="De Havilland Puss Moth">de Havilland Puss Moth</a> biplane <i>The Heart's Content</i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_20" title="August 20">August 20</a> – The Ottawa conference ends with the adoption of <a href="/wiki/Imperial_Preference" title="Imperial Preference">Imperial Preference</a> tariff, turning the British Empire into one economic zone with a series of tariffs meant to exclude non-empire states from competing within the markets of Britain; the Dominions; and the rest of the empire.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_22" title="August 22">August 22</a> – The five SA men involved in the torture and murder of Konrad Pietrzuch are quickly convicted and sentenced to death under an emergency law introduced by the Papen government on 8 August.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto1_9-1"><a href="#cite_note-auto1-9">[9]</a></sup> The Potempa case becomes a <i><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/cause_c%C3%A9l%C3%A8bre" title="wikt:cause célèbre">cause célèbre</a></i> in Germany with the Nazis demonstrating for amnesty for the "Potempa five" under the grounds they were justified in killing the Communist Pietrzuch. Hitler sends a telegram congratulating the "Potempa five".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto1_9-2"><a href="#cite_note-auto1-9">[9]</a></sup> Many Germans argue that the "Potempa five" are patriotic heroes who should not be executed while others maintain the death sentences are appropriate given the brutality of the torture and murder.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_23" title="August 23">August 23</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Civil_Aviation_Authority_(Panama)" title="Civil Aviation Authority (Panama)">Panama Civil Aviation Authority</a> is established.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_30" title="August 30">August 30</a> – <a href="/wiki/Hermann_G%C3%B6ring" title="Hermann Göring">Hermann Göring</a> is elected as Speaker of the German <i>Reichstag</i>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_31" title="August 31">August 31</a> – A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Total_solar_eclipse" title="Total solar eclipse">total solar eclipse</a> is visible from northern Canada through northeastern Vermont, New Hampshire, southwestern Maine and the Capes of Massachusetts.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="September">September</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: September">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/September_1932" title="September 1932">September 1932</a></div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_2" title="September 2">September 2</a> – Despite the court's sentence of death against the "Potempa five", Chancellor von Papen in his capacity as <i>Reich Commissioner of Prussia</i> refuses to have the "Potempa five" executed under the grounds that they were not aware of the emergency law at the time they committed the murder, but in reality because he is still hoping for Nazi support for his government.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto1_9-3"><a href="#cite_note-auto1-9">[9]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_9" title="September 9">September 9</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Cortes_Generales" title="Cortes Generales">Cortes Generales</a> (Parliament) of the <a href="/wiki/Second_Spanish_Republic" title="Second Spanish Republic">Spanish Republic</a> approved the <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Statute_of_Autonomy_of_Catalonia_of_1932&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Statute of Autonomy of Catalonia of 1932 (page does not exist)">Statute of Autonomy of Catalonia</a>, which granted full autonomy for <a href="/wiki/Catalonia" title="Catalonia">Catalonia</a> for the first time during the <a href="/wiki/Modern_history" title="Modern history">late modern period</a>.</li>
<li>Beginning of the <a href="/wiki/Chaco_War" title="Chaco War">Chaco War</a> a conflict between <a href="/wiki/Paraguay" title="Paraguay">Paraguay</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bolivia" title="Bolivia">Bolivia</a> because of delimitation problems and others.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_10" title="September 10">September 10</a> – The <a href="/wiki/IND_Eighth_Avenue_Line" title="IND Eighth Avenue Line">IND Eighth Avenue Line</a>, at this time the world's longest <a href="/wiki/Rapid_transit" title="Rapid transit">subway</a> line (31 miles (50 km)), begins operation in <a href="/wiki/Manhattan" title="Manhattan">Manhattan</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_11" title="September 11">September 11</a>
<ul>
<li>Canadian operations end on the <a href="/wiki/International_Railway_(New_York%E2%80%93Ontario)" title="International Railway (New York–Ontario)">International Railway (New York–Ontario)</a>.</li>
<li>A bronze statue of <a href="/wiki/Youssef_Bey_Karam" title="Youssef Bey Karam">Youssef Bey Karam</a> was erected in his memory outside the Cathedral of Saint Georges, <a href="/wiki/Ehden" title="Ehden">Ehden</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_12" title="September 12">September 12</a> – The very unpopular Papen government is defeated on a massive motion of no-confidence in the <i>Reichstag</i>. With the exceptions of the <a href="/wiki/German_People%27s_Party" title="German People's Party">German People's Party</a> and the <a href="/wiki/German_National_People%27s_Party" title="German National People's Party">German National People's Party</a>, every party in the <i>Reichstag</i> votes for the no-confidence motion. Papen has Hindenburg dissolve the <i>Reichstag</i> for new elections in November.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_20" title="September 20">September 20</a> – <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mohandas_K._Gandhi" title="Mohandas K. Gandhi">Mohandas K. Gandhi</a> begins a <a href="/wiki/Hunger_strike" title="Hunger strike">hunger strike</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Poona" title="Poona">Poona</a> prison, India.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_22" title="September 22">September 22</a> – <a href="/wiki/Soviet_famine_of_1932%E2%80%9333" title="Soviet famine of 1932–33">Soviet famine of 1932–33</a> begins, millions starve to death as a result of forced collectivization and as part of the government's effort to break rural resistance to its policies. The Soviet regimes denies the famine and allows millions to die.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_23" title="September 23">September 23</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Hejaz_and_Nejd" title="Kingdom of Hejaz and Nejd">Kingdom of Hejaz and Nejd</a> is proclaimed the Kingdom of <a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabia</a>, concluding the country's <a href="/wiki/Unification_of_Saudi_Arabia" title="Unification of Saudi Arabia">unification</a> under the rule of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ibn_Saud_of_Saudi_Arabia" title="Ibn Saud of Saudi Arabia">Ibn Saud</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_24" title="September 24">September 24</a> – After his party`s victory in the election to the Swedish Riksdag`s second chamber, Social Democrat <a href="/wiki/Per_Albin_Hansson" title="Per Albin Hansson">Per Albin Hansson</a> becomes the new Prime Minister of Sweden, after <a href="/wiki/Felix_Hamrin" title="Felix Hamrin">Felix Hamrin</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_27" title="September 27">September 27</a> – <a href="/wiki/Ryutin_Affair" title="Ryutin Affair">Ryutin Affair</a> at its height in the Soviet Union. The Politburo meets and condemns the so-called "Ryutin Platform" and agrees to expel those associated with it from the Communist Party, but refuses Stalin's request to execute those associated with the "Ryutin Platform".</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="October">October</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: October">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/October_1932" title="October 1932">October 1932</a></div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_1" title="October 1">October 1</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Babe_Ruth" title="Babe Ruth">Babe Ruth</a> makes his famous <a href="/wiki/Babe_Ruth%27s_called_shot" title="Babe Ruth's called shot">called shot</a> in the fifth inning of game 3 of the <a href="/wiki/1932_World_Series" title="1932 World Series">1932 World Series</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gyula_G%C3%B6mb%C3%B6s" title="Gyula Gömbös">Gyula Gömbös</a> becomes Prime Minister of Hungary, the first time a member of the radical right has become Hungary's head of government.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_3" title="October 3">October 3</a> – <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a> becomes an independent kingdom under <a href="/wiki/Faisal_I_of_Iraq" title="Faisal I of Iraq">Faisal</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_13" title="October 13">October 13</a> – Chief Justice <a href="/wiki/Charles_Evans_Hughes" title="Charles Evans Hughes">Charles Evans Hughes</a> lays the cornerstone for a new U.S. Supreme Court building.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_15" title="October 15">October 15</a>
<ul>
<li>Tata Airlines (later to become <a href="/wiki/Air_India" title="Air India">Air India</a>) makes its first flight.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Michigan_Marching_Band" title="Michigan Marching Band">Michigan Marching Band</a> (at this time called the Varsity band) debuts <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Script_Ohio" title="Script Ohio">Script Ohio</a> at the Michigan versus Ohio State game in Columbus.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_19" title="October 19">October 19</a> – <a href="/wiki/Prince_Gustaf_Adolf,_Duke_of_V%C3%A4sterbotten" title="Prince Gustaf Adolf, Duke of Västerbotten">Prince Gustav Adolf of Sweden</a> marries <a href="/wiki/Princess_Sibylla_of_Saxe-Coburg_and_Gotha" title="Princess Sibylla of Saxe-Coburg and Gotha">Princess Sibylla of Saxe-Coburg and Gotha</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_23" title="October 23">October 23</a> – <a href="/wiki/Fred_Allen" title="Fred Allen">Fred Allen</a>'s radio comedy show debuts on <a href="/wiki/CBS" title="CBS">CBS</a> in the United States.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_25" title="October 25">October 25</a> – Twenty-one-year-old Michael D'Oyly Carte, grandson of theatrical impresario and hotelier <a href="/wiki/Richard_D%27Oyly_Carte" title="Richard D'Oyly Carte">Richard D'Oyly Carte</a>, is killed in a car crash in Switzerland.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="November">November</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: November">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/November_1932" title="November 1932">November 1932</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Enigma-plugboard.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="627" data-file-width="921" height="204" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/27/Enigma-plugboard.jpg/300px-Enigma-plugboard.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/27/Enigma-plugboard.jpg/450px-Enigma-plugboard.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/27/Enigma-plugboard.jpg/600px-Enigma-plugboard.jpg 2x" width="300"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Enigma-plugboard.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Polish_Cipher_Bureau" title="Polish Cipher Bureau">Cipher Bureau</a> breaks the German Enigma cipher and overcomes the ever-growing structural and operating complexities of the evolving <a href="/wiki/Enigma_machine" title="Enigma machine">Enigma</a> with <a href="/wiki/Plugboard" title="Plugboard">plugboard</a>, the main German cipher device during World War II.</div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_1" title="November 1">November 1</a> – The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/War_Memorial_Opera_House_(San_Francisco)" title="War Memorial Opera House (San Francisco)">San Francisco Opera House</a> opens.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_3" title="November 3">November 3</a> – Strike by transport workers in Berlin. The Nazis and the Communists both co-operate in support of the strike. The Nazi-Communist co-operation hurts the Nazis at the upcoming election with many right-wing voters switching back to the <a href="/wiki/German_National_People%27s_Party" title="German National People's Party">German National People's Party</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_6" title="November 6">November 6</a> – The <a href="/wiki/German_federal_election,_November_1932" title="German federal election, November 1932"><i>Reichstag</i> election</a> is held. The Nazis remain the largest party, but their share of the seats drops from 37% to 32%.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_7" title="November 7">November 7</a> – <i><a href="/wiki/Buck_Rogers" title="Buck Rogers">Buck Rogers in the 25th Century</a></i> debuts on American <a href="/wiki/Radio" title="Radio">radio</a>. It is the first science fiction program on radio.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_8" title="November 8">November 8</a> – <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._presidential_election,_1932" title="U.S. presidential election, 1932">U.S. presidential election, 1932</a>: <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_(United_States)" title="Democratic Party (United States)">Democratic</a> Governor of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/New_York_(state)" title="New York (state)">New York</a> <a href="/wiki/Franklin_D._Roosevelt" title="Franklin D. Roosevelt">Franklin D. Roosevelt</a> defeats Republican President Herbert Hoover in a landslide victory.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_9" title="November 9">November 9</a>
<ul>
<li>A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane" title="Hurricane">hurricane</a> and huge waves kill about 2,500 in <a href="/wiki/Santa_Cruz_del_Sur" title="Santa Cruz del Sur">Santa Cruz del Sur</a> in the worst <a href="/wiki/Natural_disaster" title="Natural disaster">natural disaster</a> in <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuban</a> history.</li>
<li>Geneva massacre: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Military_of_Switzerland" title="Military of Switzerland">Military of Switzerland</a> fire on a socialist ant-fascist demonstration in <a href="/wiki/Geneva" title="Geneva">Geneva</a> leaving 13 dead and 60 injured.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_16" title="November 16">November 16</a> – New York City's <a href="/wiki/Palace_Theatre_(New_York_City)" title="Palace Theatre (New York City)">Palace Theatre</a> fully converts to a <a href="/wiki/Movie_theater" title="Movie theater">cinema</a>, which is considered the final death knell of <a href="/wiki/Vaudeville" title="Vaudeville">vaudeville</a> as a popular entertainment in the United States.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_19" title="November 19">November 19</a> – The second wife of <a href="/wiki/Joseph_Stalin" title="Joseph Stalin">Joseph Stalin</a> is found dead in her home.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_21" title="November 21">November 21</a> – German president <a href="/wiki/Paul_von_Hindenburg" title="Paul von Hindenburg">Hindenburg</a> begins negotiations with Adolf Hitler about the formation of a new government.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_24" title="November 24">November 24</a> – In Washington, D.C., the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/FBI" title="FBI">FBI</a> Scientific Crime Detection Laboratory (better known as the FBI Crime Lab) officially opens.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_30" title="November 30">November 30</a> – The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Polish_Cipher_Bureau" title="Polish Cipher Bureau">Polish Cipher Bureau</a> breaks the German <a href="/wiki/Enigma_machine" title="Enigma machine">Enigma</a> cipher.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="December">December</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: December">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/December_1932" title="December 1932">December 1932</a></div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_1" title="December 1">December 1</a> – Germany returns to the <a href="/wiki/World_Disarmament_Conference" title="World Disarmament Conference">World Disarmament Conference</a> after the others powers agree to accept <i>gleichberechtigung</i> <sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="margin-left:0.1em; white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Please_clarify" title="Wikipedia:Please clarify"><span title="The text near this tag may need clarification or removal of jargon. (December 2014)">clarification needed</span></a></i>]</sup> "in principle". Henceforward, it is clear that Germany will be allowed to rearm beyond the limits imposed by the <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Versailles" title="Treaty of Versailles">Treaty of Versailles</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_3" title="December 3">December 3</a> – Hindenburg names <a href="/wiki/Kurt_von_Schleicher" title="Kurt von Schleicher">Kurt von Schleicher</a> as German chancellor after he ousts Papen. Papen is deeply angry about how his former friend Schleicher has brought him down and decides that he will do anything to get back into power.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_4" title="December 4">December 4</a> – Chancellor Schleicher meets with <a href="/wiki/Gregor_Strasser" title="Gregor Strasser">Gregor Strasser</a> and offers to appoint him Vice-Chancellor and <i>Reich</i> Commissioner for Prussia out of the hope that if faced with a split in the NSDAP, Hitler will support his government.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_5" title="December 5">December 5</a> – At a secret meeting of the Nazi leaders, Strasser urges Hitler to drop his "all or nothing" strategy and accept Schleicher's offer to have the Nazis serve in his cabinet.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto3_17-0"><a href="#cite_note-auto3-17">[17]</a></sup> Hitler gives a dramatic speech saying that Schleicher's offer is not acceptable and he will stick to his "all or nothing" strategy whatever the consequences might be and wins the Nazi leadership over to his viewpoint.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto3_17-1"><a href="#cite_note-auto3-17">[17]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_8" title="December 8">December 8</a> – <a href="/wiki/Gregor_Strasser" title="Gregor Strasser">Gregor Strasser</a> resigns as the chief of the NSDAP's organizational department in protest against Hitler's "all or nothing" strategy.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_12" title="December 12">December 12</a> – Japan and the <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">Soviet Union</a> reform their diplomatic connections.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="margin-left:0.1em; white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Please_clarify" title="Wikipedia:Please clarify"><span title="The text near this tag may need clarification or removal of jargon. (December 2016)">clarification needed</span></a></i>]</sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_19" title="December 19">December 19</a> – <a href="/wiki/BBC_World_Service" title="BBC World Service">BBC World Service</a> begins broadcasting as the BBC Empire Service.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_23" title="December 23">December 23</a> or <a href="/wiki/December_24" title="December 24">24</a> – A methane gas explosion causes the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Moweaqua_Coal_Mine_Disaster" title="Moweaqua Coal Mine Disaster">Moweaqua Coal Mine Disaster</a> which claims 54 lives.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_25" title="December 25">December 25</a>
<ul>
<li>The 7.6 <a href="/wiki/Surface_wave_magnitude" title="Surface wave magnitude">Ms</a> <a href="/wiki/1932_Changma_earthquake" title="1932 Changma earthquake">Changma earthquake</a> shakes the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kansu" title="Kansu">Kansu Province</a> in China with a maximum <a href="/wiki/Mercalli_intensity_scale" title="Mercalli intensity scale">Mercalli intensity</a> of X (<i>Extreme</i>). Two-hundred and seventy-five people were killed.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/IG_Farben" title="IG Farben">IG Farben</a> file a <a href="/wiki/Patent" title="Patent">patent</a> application in Germany for the medical application of the first <a href="/wiki/Sulfonamide_(medicine)" title="Sulfonamide (medicine)">sulfonamide</a> oral <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Antibiotic" title="Antibiotic">antibiotic</a>, which will be marketed as <a href="/wiki/Prontosil" title="Prontosil">Prontosil</a>, following <a href="/wiki/Gerhard_Domagk" title="Gerhard Domagk">Gerhard Domagk</a>'s laboratory demonstration of its properties as an antibiotic.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19"><a href="#cite_note-19">[19]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_27" title="December 27">December 27</a> –
<ul>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Radio_City_Music_Hall" title="Radio City Music Hall">Radio City Music Hall</a></i> opens in New York City.</li>
<li>Internal passports are introduced in the Soviet Union.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_28" title="December 28">December 28</a> – The Cologne banker <a href="/wiki/Kurt_Baron_von_Schr%C3%B6der" title="Kurt Baron von Schröder">Kurt von Schröder</a>-who is a close friend of Papen and a NSDAP member-meets with <a href="/wiki/Adolf_Hitler" title="Adolf Hitler">Adolf Hitler</a> to tell him that Papen wants to set up a meeting to discuss how they can work together. Papen wants Nazi support to return to the Chancellorship while Hitler wants Papen to convince Hindenburg to appoint him Chancellor. Hitler agrees to meet Papen on 3 January 1933.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Date_unknown">Date unknown</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Date unknown">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:The_Adventures_of_Tintin_-_03_-_Tintin_in_America.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="396" data-file-width="300" height="290" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/90/The_Adventures_of_Tintin_-_03_-_Tintin_in_America.jpg/220px-The_Adventures_of_Tintin_-_03_-_Tintin_in_America.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/9/90/The_Adventures_of_Tintin_-_03_-_Tintin_in_America.jpg 1.5x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:The_Adventures_of_Tintin_-_03_-_Tintin_in_America.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Date unknown: <a href="/wiki/Herg%C3%A9" title="Hergé">Hergé</a>'s <i><a href="/wiki/Tintin_in_America" title="Tintin in America">Tintin in America</a></i> is published in black and white</div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dust_storm" title="Dust storm">Dust storms</a> begin in <a href="/wiki/Kansas" title="Kansas">Kansas</a>, <a href="/wiki/Oklahoma" title="Oklahoma">Oklahoma</a>, <a href="/wiki/Colorado" title="Colorado">Colorado</a>, <a href="/wiki/New_Mexico" title="New Mexico">New Mexico</a> and <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">Texas</a>, the start of the <a href="/wiki/Dust_Bowl" title="Dust Bowl">Dust Bowl</a> in the United States.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20"><a href="#cite_note-20">[20]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Zippo" title="Zippo">Zippo</a> lighters are developed.</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Zero-length_spring" title="Zero-length spring">Zero-length springs</a> are invented, revolutionizing <a href="/wiki/Seismometer" title="Seismometer">seismometers</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gravimeter" title="Gravimeter">gravimeters</a>.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Kennedy%E2%80%93Thorndike_experiment" title="Kennedy–Thorndike experiment">Kennedy–Thorndike experiment</a> shows that measured time as well as length are affected by motion, in accordance with the theory of <a href="/wiki/Special_relativity" title="Special relativity">special relativity</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/James_Chadwick" title="James Chadwick">James Chadwick</a> discovers the <a href="/wiki/Neutron" title="Neutron">neutron</a>.</li>
<li>Geneticist <a href="/wiki/J._B._S._Haldane" title="J. B. S. Haldane">J. B. S. Haldane</a> publishes <i>The Causes of Evolution</i>, unifying the findings of Mendelian <a href="/wiki/Genetics" title="Genetics">genetics</a> with those of <a href="/wiki/Evolution" title="Evolution">evolutionary</a> science.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Heath_hen" title="Heath hen">heath hen</a> becomes extinct in North America.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Walter_B._Pitkin" title="Walter B. Pitkin">Walter B. Pitkin</a> publishes <i><a href="/wiki/Life_Begins_at_Forty" title="Life Begins at Forty">Life Begins at Forty</a></i> in the United States.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Republican_Citizens_Committee_Against_National_Prohibition" title="Republican Citizens Committee Against National Prohibition">Republican Citizens Committee Against National Prohibition</a> is established for the <a href="/wiki/Repeal_of_Prohibition_in_the_United_States" title="Repeal of Prohibition in the United States">repeal of Prohibition in the United States</a>.</li>
<li>Yezd <a href="/wiki/Fire_temple" title="Fire temple">Fire temple</a> (<i>Atash Behram</i>) becomes established in <a href="/wiki/Yazd" title="Yazd">Yazd</a>, Iran.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Association_for_Research_and_Enlightenment" title="Association for Research and Enlightenment">Association for Research and Enlightenment</a>, Inc. (ARE) founded in Virginia Beach, Virginia, as an open-membership group to research the collected transcripts of <a href="/wiki/Edgar_Cayce" title="Edgar Cayce">Edgar Cayce</a>'s continuing trances, stored at the Edgar Cayce Foundation.</li>
<li>"The Noah of Washington Mud Flats" predicts a Deluge in 1936, building an <a href="/wiki/Noah%27s_Ark" title="Noah's Ark">Ark</a> and demon-proof armor.</li>
<li>Unemployment in the United States – ca. 33% – 14 million. A similar level of unemployment affects Germany. Many people in depressed countries do not receive unemployment benefit due to governments not being able to afford benefit payments.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21"><a href="#cite_note-21">[21]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Herg%C3%A9" title="Hergé">Hergé</a>'s <i><a href="/wiki/Tintin_in_America" title="Tintin in America">Tintin in America</a></i> is published in black and white.</li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Births">Births</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Births">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="March_2">March</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: March">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Ryszard_Kapuscinski_by_Kubik_17.05.1997.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="480" data-file-width="393" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/07/Ryszard_Kapuscinski_by_Kubik_17.05.1997.jpg/120px-Ryszard_Kapuscinski_by_Kubik_17.05.1997.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/07/Ryszard_Kapuscinski_by_Kubik_17.05.1997.jpg/180px-Ryszard_Kapuscinski_by_Kubik_17.05.1997.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/07/Ryszard_Kapuscinski_by_Kubik_17.05.1997.jpg/240px-Ryszard_Kapuscinski_by_Kubik_17.05.1997.jpg 2x" width="120"/></a>

<a href="/wiki/Ryszard_Kapu%C5%9Bci%C5%84ski" title="Ryszard Kapuściński">Ryszard Kapuściński</a></div>

<li><a href="/wiki/August_24" title="August 24">August 24</a> – <a href="/wiki/Kate_M._Gordon" title="Kate M. Gordon">Kate M. Gordon</a>, American suffragette (b. <a href="/wiki/1861" title="1861">1861</a>)</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="September_3">September</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: September">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_5" title="September 5">September 5</a> – <a href="/wiki/Paul_Bern" title="Paul Bern">Paul Bern</a>, American screenwriter (b. <a href="/wiki/1889" title="1889">1889</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_8" title="September 8">September 8</a> – <a href="/wiki/Christian_von_Ehrenfels" title="Christian von Ehrenfels">Christian von Ehrenfels</a>, Austrian philosopher (b. <a href="/wiki/1859" title="1859">1859</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_10" title="September 10">September 10</a> – <a href="/wiki/Huey_Long" title="Huey Long">Huey Long</a>, Assassinated American politician, 40th <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Governor_of_Louisiana" title="Governor of Louisiana">Governor of Louisiana</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_Senator" title="United States Senator">United States Senator</a> from <a href="/wiki/Louisiana" title="Louisiana">Louisiana</a> (b. <a href="/wiki/1893" title="1893">1893</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_16" title="September 16">September 16</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Ross" title="Ronald Ross">Ronald Ross</a>, English physician, recipient of the <a href="/wiki/Nobel_Prize_in_Physiology_or_Medicine" title="Nobel Prize in Physiology or Medicine">Nobel Prize in Physiology or Medicine</a> (b. <a href="/wiki/1857" title="1857">1857</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Peg_Entwistle" title="Peg Entwistle">Peg Entwistle</a>, film actress (b. <a href="/wiki/1908" title="1908">1908</a>)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_20" title="September 20">September 20</a> – <a href="/wiki/Wovoka" title="Wovoka">Wovoka</a>, Paiute visionary (<i>Ghost Dance</i>) (b. c. <a href="/wiki/1856" title="1856">1856</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_23" title="September 23">September 23</a> – <a href="/wiki/Jules_Ch%C3%A9ret" title="Jules Chéret">Jules Chéret</a>, French poster designer (b. <a href="/wiki/1836" title="1836">1836</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_25" title="September 25">September 25</a> – <a href="/wiki/Joel_R._P._Pringle" title="Joel R. P. Pringle">Joel R. P. Pringle</a>, American admiral (b. <a href="/wiki/1873" title="1873">1873</a>)</li>
</ul>

<li id="cite_note-21"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-21">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a class="external text" href="http://www.historyhome.co.uk/europe/weimar.htm" rel="nofollow">US unemployment statistics</a>, historyhome.co.uk; accessed December 10, 2014.</span></li>
</ol>
